\subsection{Detailed Description}
Miscenalleous\+: logs, version strings, config storage. 



\subsection{Typedef Documentation}
\mbox{\label{group__misc_gaf621181934fa2be96ebb2b498fc59cff}} 
\index{Misc@{Misc}!Linphone\+Config@{Linphone\+Config}}
\index{Linphone\+Config@{Linphone\+Config}!Misc@{Misc}}
\subsubsection{Linphone\+Config}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef struct \+\_\+\+Lp\+Config \textbf{ Linphone\+Config}}



The Linphone\+Config object is used to manipulate a configuration file. 

The format of the configuration file is a .ini like format\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item sections are defined in []
\item each section contains a sequence of key=value pairs.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
[sound]
echocanceler=1
playback\_dev=ALSA: Default device

[video]
enabled=1
\end{DoxyCode}
 \mbox{\label{group__misc_ga8f3b35ce44e1284465ac2859ffbb9db7}} 
\index{Misc@{Misc}!Linphone\+Error\+Info@{Linphone\+Error\+Info}}
\index{Linphone\+Error\+Info@{Linphone\+Error\+Info}!Misc@{Misc}}
\subsubsection{Linphone\+Error\+Info}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef struct \+\_\+\+Linphone\+Error\+Info \textbf{ Linphone\+Error\+Info}}



Object representing full details about a signaling error or status. 

All Linphone\+Error\+Info object returned by the liblinphone A\+PI are readonly and transcients. For safety they must be used immediately after obtaining them. Any other function call to the liblinphone may change their content or invalidate the pointer. \mbox{\label{group__misc_ga52469d4a84233345d8dfa8c300aa98f9}} 
\index{Misc@{Misc}!Linphone\+Headers@{Linphone\+Headers}}
\index{Linphone\+Headers@{Linphone\+Headers}!Misc@{Misc}}
\subsubsection{Linphone\+Headers}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef struct \+\_\+\+Linphone\+Headers \textbf{ Linphone\+Headers}}



Object representing a chain of protocol headers. 

It provides read/write access to the headers of the underlying protocol. \mbox{\label{group__misc_ga6c15f2fecbd38cd7a226a1b1fac82afc}}

Retrieves a configuration item as a list of strings, given its section, key, and default value. 

The default value is returned if the config item is not found.

\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+config\+\_\+new\+\_\+with\+\_\+factory()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \textbf{ Linphone\+Config}$\ast$ linphone\+\_\+config\+\_\+new\+\_\+with\+\_\+factory (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{config\+\_\+filename,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{factory\+\_\+config\+\_\+filename }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Instantiates a Linphone\+Config object from a user config file and a factory config file. 

The caller of this constructor owns a reference. \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+config\+\_\+unref()}{p.}{group__misc_ga2e41ac27f6189f0fc7b06f765ed1132a} must be called when this object is no longer needed.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em config\+\_\+filename} & the filename of the user config file to read to fill the instantiated Linphone\+Config \\
\hline
{\em factory\+\_\+config\+\_\+filename} & the filename of the factory config file to read to fill the instantiated Linphone\+Config \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxyref{linphone\+\_\+config\+\_\+new}{p.}{group__misc_gab7bf012f25eb4ff087f11dddaff546fd}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
The user config file is read first to fill the Linphone\+Config and then the factory config file is read. Therefore the configuration parameters defined in the user config file will be overwritten by the parameters defined in the factory config file. \mbox{\label{group__misc_ga33e6109792c4329c323f227e85352d49}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \textbf{ Linphone\+Status} linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+play\+\_\+local (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{audiofile }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Plays an audio file to the local user. 

This function works at any time, during calls, or when no calls are running. It doesn\textquotesingle{}t request the underlying audio system to support multiple playback streams. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em lc} & Linphone\+Core object \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em audiofile} & The path to an audio file in wav P\+CM 16 bit format \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success, -\/1 on error 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \textbf{ Linphone\+Status} linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+take\+\_\+preview\+\_\+snapshot (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{file }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Take a photo of currently from capture device and write it into a jpeg file. 

Note that the snapshot is asynchronous, an application shall not assume that the file is created when the function returns.

\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{Misc@{Misc}!linphone\+\_\+error\+\_\+info\+\_\+new@{linphone\+\_\+error\+\_\+info\+\_\+new}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+error\+\_\+info\+\_\+new@{linphone\+\_\+error\+\_\+info\+\_\+new}!Misc@{Misc}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+error\+\_\+info\+\_\+new()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \textbf{ Linphone\+Error\+Info}$\ast$ linphone\+\_\+error\+\_\+info\+\_\+new (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Create an empty Linphone\+Error\+Info object. 

The Linphone\+Error\+Info object carries these fields\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item a Linphone\+Reason enum member giving overall signification of the error reported.
\item the \char`\"{}protocol\char`\"{} name in which the protocol reason code has meaning, for example S\+IP or Q.\+850
\item the \char`\"{}protocol code\char`\"{}, an integer referencing the kind of error reported
\item the \char`\"{}phrase\char`\"{}, a text phrase describing the error
\item the \char`\"{}warning\char`\"{}, the content of warning headers if any
\item a sub \char`\"{}\+Linphone\+Error\+Info\char`\"{} may be provided if a S\+IP response includes a Reason header (R\+F\+C3326). 
\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\label{group__misc_ga2408d6a06eeb6eea580178274ea75a6f}} 
\index{Misc@{Misc}!linphone\+\_\+error\+\_\+info\+\_\+ref@{linphone\+\_\+error\+\_\+info\+\_\+ref}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+error\+\_\+info\+\_\+ref@{linphone\+\_\+error\+\_\+info\+\_\+ref}!Misc@{Misc}}

\index{Misc@{Misc}!linphone\+\_\+error\+\_\+info\+\_\+set\+\_\+sub\+\_\+error\+\_\+info@{linphone\+\_\+error\+\_\+info\+\_\+set\+\_\+sub\+\_\+error\+\_\+info}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+error\+\_\+info\+\_\+set\+\_\+sub\+\_\+error\+\_\+info@{linphone\+\_\+error\+\_\+info\+\_\+set\+\_\+sub\+\_\+error\+\_\+info}!Misc@{Misc}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+error\+\_\+info\+\_\+set\+\_\+sub\+\_\+error\+\_\+info()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void linphone\+\_\+error\+\_\+info\+\_\+set\+\_\+sub\+\_\+error\+\_\+info (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Error\+Info} $\ast$}]{ei,  }\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Error\+Info} $\ast$}]{appended\+\_\+ei }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the sub\+\_\+ei in Linphone\+Error\+Info to another Linphone\+Error\+Info. 

Used when a reason header is to be added in a S\+IP response. The first level Linphone\+Error\+Info defines the S\+IP response code and phrase, the second (sub) Linphone\+Erro\+Info defining the content of the Reason header. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em ei} & Linphone\+Error\+Info object to which the other Linphone\+Error\+Info will be appended as ei-\/$>$sub\+\_\+ei. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em appended\+\_\+ei} & Linphone\+Error\+Info to append \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
